The 8th God's Day Message
Until now, human history has revolved around the Cain and Abel issue…. The whole must unite to pave the way centered on the Messiah, and when we connect individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world all at once, we can fulfill God's will within the 7-year period. This is God's will. 
God's Will for Us During the 2nd 7-Year Course
To fulfill this will, God established Judaism and the Israelite nation. Furthermore, to lay the foundation for connecting this standard globally during the Last Days of the Second Advent, He established Christianity and the democratic world. The era of Jesus and the present time differ in spiritual standards. Now is a global era, while the era of the Israelite nation, centered on Judaism, was a national era. The dimension has changed. God's will is to settle everything within this 7-year process.
Our Unification Church has been centered on the teacher until now, but because Christianity could not unite on the Cain and Abel standard, the teacher is making external preparations again. In other words, because Jesus could not fulfill the mission of the Messiah, he is re-establishing the foundation of John the Baptist, connecting it to the foundation of the Messiah, and must restore the position of Cain and Abel to take the place of parents. We must go this way again. Therefore, the teacher has walked the path of suffering in faith until now, receiving opposition from Christianity.
From the perspective of the teacher's life, until the age of 40, he was centered on the standard of personal victory, and it was the time to transition to a horizontal foundation. The 1960s was a time when the purpose of the restoration history was to establish one Adam, and it was a time to lay the foundation for Adam to be victorious. What kind of victory is this? It refers to victory based on the national standard where Jesus failed. Therefore, in the 1960s, our Unification Church had to substantially indemnify the realm of destiny where Jesus inevitably had to fail, based on the teacher's age of 40. During that process, our Unification Church faced tremendous persecution in the 1960s. If the teacher had not made the decisive pledge to discern good and evil as a human before God out of lack of courage, history would have been delayed.
However, despite all hardships…. It was just like the scene when Jesus was crucified. The number of central figures opposing him was exactly the same as those who followed Jesus. Three people opposed, twelve united to oppose, and the entire nation and religion launched a total attack, facing the final suffocating crisis, making a decisive resolution to overcome death. Thus, he established the foundation for personal victory and expanded the horizontal foundation. Consequently, a national transformation was achieved in the 1960s.
What does the horizontal foundation mean? It means expanding the relative foothold centered on Adam. What standards exist in this horizontal foundation? There is the faith of the newborn, the faith of the grown, and the faith of completion, and there is also the reality of the newborn, grown, and completed, and in heart…. This is how it works.
From this perspective, the period of connecting a mother to a completed male is the 7-year course. What is this 7-year course? It is the period of establishing the teacher's family standard. Therefore, at that time, a family was formed centered on God. It was then that the restoration form of the son-in-law expectation was established, creating a family point on earth.
9
Then, centered on the teacher's family, what must be done? Blessed families must unite completely. They must become one centered on the family, and this period is the 2nd 7-year course. What is the 2nd 7-year course? It is the period in which the blessed families centered on the teacher's family become completely one. This must become completely one to become an Abel realm and restore the national standard.
Then, what does the united family correspond to? If we look at it centered on the Israelite nation, it is in the same position as the family of Jesus, the twelve apostles, the seventy disciples, and all the patriarchs of Israel being able to unite. There should be no objection to this.
Because of such issues in reality, the 2nd 7-year course is the period in which the teacher's family and blessed families become one. What must they do when they become one? They must carry out national indemnity. However, many of you have often followed your own circumstances. Did anyone who came out know that they were in an intermediate position responsible for the national mission centered on God's will and the teacher? No, there was not. Thus, those who do not know have raised various doubts, opposed, and caused much confusion centered on the standard that should unite. Therefore, this had to be indemnified and overcome.
Victory Foundation for the 3rd 7-Year Course
For this reason, in 1970, families mobilized centered on the teacher. Thus, to indemnify what could not be united, they had to go through the 3-year course while holding onto the nation and shedding tears. Therefore, blessed families entrusted their children to parents who opposed them, such as orphanages or various fields, and the blessed family children stood in a position of carrying the cross, experiencing loneliness and shedding tears. At that time, among those who had opposed until now, such as members of established churches or people of the nation, although they disliked the Unification Church, there were groups who could not help but love the children of the Unification Church, holding the motherless children and shedding tears. 
10   The 8th God's Day Message
You may not know, but there must have been such people around you.
Thus, the church people or the people of the nation indemnified their opposition to God and became a point where the families of the Korean people could follow the teacher's family and your families to connect the family standard to the spiritual standard. It cannot be done on a physical standard.
If you stood in a position to fulfill the will centered on a physical standard, this would be a complete failure. Because it was a spiritual standard, it was a spiritual restoration process where one could go out, return, repent, and go out again. Thus, through the 3-year course of family persecution or the 3-year course of sacrifice, conditions were established for this nation to reconnect before God spiritually. What does this mean? It means that the conditions for the national standard to connect with our families have been established. 
You must understand this. Through that foundation, the teacher had to go toward the global 3rd 7-year course, and from 1972 to 1974, he had to absorb the spiritual foundation of Christianity globally and set a central direction there.
Therefore, although there was persecution in Korea, there should not be persecution on the global stage. Thus, while being attacked in Korea, based on the principle of indemnity and restoration, on the global stage, I attacked, and by not retreating, not being pushed back, I stood in a decisive position where everyone recognized, ‘Ah, Reverend Moon has triumphed.’ This established a standard where I could fully absorb the spiritual foundation of the Christian world. By uniting American youth and youth from the Western world, I completely finished the foundation that could move a national fortune and reconnect the entire nation through the 3-year course victoriously. Thus, I smoothly passed the 2nd 7-year course and returned this time to welcome the 3rd 7-year course, allowing us to leave a realm centered not only on the spiritual but also on the physical. 
You must understand that, from a principled perspective, it was not from the 2nd 7-year course that we ascended. In other words, it is from Adam and Eve. From this perspective, we must restore all of humanity. Whose sons and daughters are humanity? Of course, they are the sons and daughters of fallen Adam. Therefore, to restore, there must be an unfallen Adam and an unfallen Eve besides the fallen sons and daughters of Adam. This is why the standard of the bride and groom arises in the era of the Second Advent.
From this perspective, when we look at the Unification Church itself, you must understand that it is essential to be loyal in supporting the mother from the time of the newborn 7-year course until the time of the grown 7-year course. Why? Because there must be a woman who plays a leading role in indemnifying all that Eve failed in, carrying all the crosses of personal, family…. Every cross must be borne before the Father. The central figure who has played that role until now has been Teacher Choi. This cannot just be pushed forward as it is principled. Why? Because the completion level must be crossed by a couple, two people. It is a path for two people.
Now is the time for us to ascend.
Having passed the 2nd 7-year course, from now on, we must focus on the Father and Mother in the 3rd 7-year course. Until now, Teacher Choi has worked hard to lay the foundation for the mother, which you do not know. You must understand that it was on that foundation that the 2nd 7-year course was smoothly overcome. However, from now on, more than anyone else, you must take the position of a dutiful daughter who serves the mother and walk a difficult path to establish heavenly law.
In this sense, I hope you will provide much comfort and support both spiritually and externally. Of course, the teacher must also be taken out, but above all, while individual circumstances are important, we must establish a public position for the sake of the will. Therefore, even if an individual experiences sorrow, for the sake of public joy, one must make a decisive resolution and move forward. This is the path the teacher has walked until now and the path of the restoration providence.
Knowing this, you should appreciate that you have come this far through Teacher Choi's efforts and hope that you will move forward with even more vigor. Let’s welcome with applause. (Applause)
Now, I will conclude with this today. Are there no questions? “About the 3rd 7-Year Course….” In the 3rd 7-Year Course, the satanic world descends and we ascend. This will happen personally and also in families from now on. The satanic world will descend…. Until now, since the spiritual standard has been the world standard, it could not descend. It could not descend because the fortune of the spiritual standard had not been indemnified. However, now is the time to descend both spiritually and physically. Therefore, the world will descend and we will ascend.
For this reason, during this 3-year period, although there are many Unification Church members in America or worldwide, the number is not the issue. The issue is to become completely one. If we unite completely without any objections in the will, remarkable results will appear from now on when you do something. From now on, our efforts will not be subject to the principle of indemnity; they will remain on God's side, on the side of goodness. Do you understand? “Yes.” That’s right, isn’t it, principled? Because we must raise the fortune that has descended, we have gone up and down for 6,000 years. We have now surpassed that.
Therefore, the teacher must overcome this new hurdle centered on the UN issue or the Korean issue. This cannot be done on a national standard. Also, the realm that the Messiah must go to is a horizontal stage, not a vertical stage. Therefore, finally, after the teacher turned 50, he appeared in an official position in the world to address the public and hold such a gathering. This is the first time, right?
We must re-establish the foundation that Jesus could not lay during his 3-year course from a spiritual standard. Because Jesus died. In looking at this, God is the King of Wisdom. Because Jesus died, having to indemnify the path again, the flesh was struck, but the spirit was not struck, so all were spiritually saved if they repented.
13
From now on, such times will pass. Until now, much has been forgiven, but gradually…. Once we pass the 7-year course of the completion era, the era of direct law will come. At that time, there will be no forgiveness.
Now, since we are heading toward that point, being within the realm of the principle of the completion era, who must play the leading role? In the family, Adam must play the leading role. Because we must manage the world, from now on, let’s gradually move in the direction of managing world issues. In the future, it will become increasingly chaotic, but the Unification Church will maintain its posture and clarify its purpose, navigating through the direction, so many people will come to ask. Anyone curious will ask, “What will happen? How should we go?” From now on, due to the global storm, a new global system will arise, centered on the environments of the newborn and grown…. The 3rd 7-Year Course is centered on the newborn, grown, and completed.
In this process, when is the realm of the newborn? It is the 3-year substantial course. When is the realm of the grown? It is the following 3 years. Together, that makes 6 years. Therefore, when we add the 7, we see that we move into the realm of completion. If we divide this, we can see it as the first 3 years, the following 3 years, and then when we add up to 7, it is 7 years. If we look at the 7-year period as two parts, we can divide it into the first 3 and the following 3. Thus, in the first 3-year period, we lay the foundation for the spiritual world, and in the following 3-year period, we align the foundation for the substantial world. On the day this is completed, then liberation will come. In this era, God will remove all those who oppose us, all those who stand against our will. The time will come when God will act. Isn’t that so? Now is such a time.
Having come this far, we must strive until the 7-year course beyond the substantial 3-year course…. That is until 1981, right? We must work hard until 1981. This is the most breathless time…. While the external world may point fingers, what the Unification Church pursues will unfold. A hopeful world will come. The transitional period is this 3-year period.
Yes, do you understand? "Yes." It will undoubtedly become such a world. It must be that way. Even if you try to suffer in the future, there will be no way to suffer. Therefore, I believe we must proceed swiftly. Knowing this, you must ensure that you do not lose the dignity, face, and authority of the subject nation in front of the world, starting with the unity of the 36 families, the unity of the 72 families, and the unity of the entire family...

You are experiencing something that happens only once in the eternal historical journey. You must understand that you are doing something that is historically unprecedented.

**The Significance of God's Day and the Significance of the Third 7-Year Course**

Today, as you all know, is the eighth God's Day. It is also a historic day as we embark on the Third 7-Year Course. So today, I will briefly speak about "the significance of God's Day and the significance of the Third 7-Year Course."

**The Content of Salvation Providence in the Process of Fulfilling God's Will**

We know that due to the fall, the world where God's sovereignty can be established, where God can govern and direct as He wishes, has not been realized. However, because God is eternal, His will is one and cannot be two. Since it is God's position that His eternal will must be fulfilled as an unchanging will, even though there was a fall, there is a movement to find it again. This return does not happen just by chance; it must go through certain principles, which is why we understand that it comes through a process of recreation.

When Adam and Eve fell, the archangel, Adam, and Eve became one. This standard is not only a problem that occurred at that time during the fall in Eden, but it is also a historical issue.

When an event occurs between one person and another, it does not end with just those two people; it must involve witnesses or one side must become involved, leading to a chain reaction. This creates a relationship where it either continues on the side of evil or on the side of good.

However, when we look at Adam and Eve's fall, it resulted in the side of evil. Thus, the purpose for which God created Adam, the purpose for which He created Eve, and the purpose for which He created the angels remain unfulfilled. Therefore, this must be restored, and the historical religion has taken on the mission of this restoration. The meaning of salvation providence originally did not exist within God's providence; it is in an intermediate position, standing in a transitional period to return from the fallen world back to God. Because this still remains, we must understand that religion is still in the process of pursuing an unachieved goal.

Therefore, this entire religion, which is in the process of salvation providence, must be resolved, and we must complete the salvation providence and transition to the original world of God's will where salvation providence is no longer needed. For this, who must be the responsible person to make this transition? It must be someone better than Adam. Adam was the one responsible for transitioning from God's world to the world of Satan. However, that Adam was an incomplete Adam. Because he could not become a complete Adam, he could not fulfill God's will. Therefore, to fulfill the will, a complete Adam must be reappeared. Only then can we return to the world of the will.

Returning to the world of the will requires us to gather all the mainstream religions of the salvation providence and all the related religions to turn back. This is the content of the salvation providence in the process of fulfilling God's will.

Originally, we did not need religion. Religion is not necessary where the original will is fulfilled, where God's desires are realized. We should simply recognize God as our Father within His love and be governed as His sons and daughters, and then establish one family of God, tribes, nations, and the world. Therefore, if this is not restored, the world that God desires cannot be realized. This is the essence of salvation providence.

So, what position are we in now? We are in the process of salvation providence. Are we just going to push this process of salvation providence in a flat manner? No. It must develop step by step.

Today, according to our principle, we must go through the stages of the revival of the Old Testament era, the growth of the New Testament era, and the completion of the Completed Testament era to establish the standard of the will that should have been realized without the fall. At the point of agreement of that will, I must be in harmony with God's heart, in harmony with God's body, and in harmony with all of God's creation. In other words, God must be the master of our human hearts, and we must move according to God's control, not according to our own desires.

**The Day God Loves Most is God's Day**

Today, fallen humanity cannot do this. Because we are transitioning into such a world, the issue of possession has become a major problem today. As you know, whether it is a capitalist society or a communist society, it revolves around the issue of possession. Should we focus on individual ownership or state ownership? From the perspective of God's will, you must understand that focusing on state ownership is closer to the will than individual ownership. The evil Satan first understood this and has taken the path of communal ownership from individual ownership. Excluding God, that play is communism. 

The material I possess is communal property, and my body is also communal property. This is how it is. Then what happens to my heart? The heart is also communal property. It is not a communal property without direction or purpose. It connects the ownership that can completely align the purpose of the subject and object centered on God.

When this happens, what is the result? In the end, I possess God. I come to possess God. When I possess God instead of material, I possess the complete subject of all material, the complete subject of our human bodies, and then the complete subject of our hearts. When I possess God, I possess the subjective standard that can own everything. Therefore, when I become one with Him, that position becomes qualified to face everything. You must understand that this is the fundamental principle of the creation of heaven and earth.

Now, when we look at the Unification Church today, it observes the four major holidays: Parents' Day, Children's Day, All Things Day, and God's Day. Those who do not believe do not understand this. Today, those who do not know this content might say, "The Unification Church has Parents' Day, but don't we have parents? What kind of Parents' Day is that? And do we not have children? What kind of Children's Day is that? And they say it is All Things Day, but is there nothing?" They will not understand at all.

The parents you know today, or the children, or the possessions you have are not returned to God; they are just parents, siblings, or children who have inherited the traditions of Satan within the realm of Satan. However, there have been no parents returned to God, no children returned to God, and no all things returned to God.

So what is God's Day? What is God's Day? It is the day when God completes the ideal of creation.

Now, we humans also commemorate our birthdays, calling the day we were born our birthday. We can say that the day we were born is a truly joyful day. However, while successful and happy people may consider their birthday a joyous day, those who experience continuous misfortune may lament the fact that their parents gave birth to them. Furthermore, what is the day that should be commemorated for humans? It is the wedding day, the day of marriage. What is the happiest day for humans? The day of birth is something one does not know. When one is born as a baby, what joy is there?

What is the happiest day for humans? It is the day when a man, having grown up, meets a woman, and a woman meets a man to marry, that is, the day they pass through the gateway of love. Even in the fallen world, this is acknowledged.

There is also the saying that a virgin who dies without ever marrying becomes a vengeful spirit. If one dies without ever having been married, it is said that they become a vengeful spirit filled with regret. That saying is indeed true.

When we consider this, what standard did God establish for the day that can bring the greatest joy to humans? Of course, the day of birth is a joyful day. But at that time, one is a baby and does not know. Therefore, the most precious day for humans is the day of marriage. Do you understand?

There may be older virgins and older bachelors here. Those over 30 may have been saying "marriage, marriage" without getting married, and they often feel exhausted, not knowing whether it is a house of marriage or a house of spirits. They need to get married, right? (Laughter) Everyone is laughing.

Young ladies, as you grow up, you may be putting on makeup and trying to be a refined lady... walking around like a little bird. Why do you go around? It would be nice to just sit quietly. There are times when you go out for no reason. Why is that? It is because you are looking for a partner. (Laughter) Why are you laughing? Am I lying?

And young men over 20, when they reach that age, they used to look in one direction, but once they turn 20, their eyes start wandering. When a girl walks by, they might make a sound... (Laughter) Why do they do that? Is it because they are bad or because they are good? "It is because they are good." Yes, that's right. (Laughter)

So, looking at this, what is the happiest thing for a happy person? It is for a man and a woman to get married. Today, I am not talking about marriage between men and women, but that is how it is. Among the flowers of life, marriage is the flower of flowers, the fragrance of fragrances, and the only way to pursue the valuable fruits of our lives.

**Our Father is the Best**

So, do you want to be a happy person? Do you want to have a happy family? People prefer a happy family over just being happy, right? Even if one is happy because they have a lot of money, knowledge, or power, without a spouse, that is all there is to it. (Laughter) That young lady is so happy... (Laughter) This man... anyway, it is good. If you are that happy from the first day of the lunar new year, blessings will come. (Laughter and applause)

Now, when we think of the holy, holy God, who is the Lord of heaven and earth, what do you think He would like? Money? He can create money as much as He wants. Power? God is omnipotent, so what good is power? Knowledge? God created the source of all principles in heaven and earth; does He need that? He is the king of knowledge, the great king of power, and the king of money. What does He need? Do you think God looks at money and says, "Oh, how nice!"? Do you think He looks at power and says, "Oh, how nice!"? Do you think He looks at knowledge and says, "Oh, how great I am!"?

Now, imagine a president of a country who is well-equipped in every aspect and renowned worldwide. When that president goes to a cabinet meeting and commands, "Hey, I am going to run the world with this purpose and this content, so you all do this," does that president feel happy when everyone says, "Yes, we will do that"? No, there is no change in that situation. However, when he comes home tired after a long day, and his cute little child comes running and says, "Daddy!" does he use his power then? There is no need for power there, right? Is money needed? There is no need for knowledge, money, or power there. When the child says, "Daddy!" he responds, "Yes, yes." When the child says, "Daddy!" does he say, "Hmm!"? No, he says, "Yes, yes." Even if his eyes are wrinkled and his face is full of lines, he will say, "Yes! Yes!" No matter how high he is, he will bend down and say, "Oh, my child!" That is how it is.

When we look at this, it cannot be helped. God is the same. When God created humans, what did He do it for? Not just to play with them, but to show them something fun, to show us that our Father is great. He wants to show us everything that our Father does well. Wouldn't that be the case? Then the child would say, "My father is the best. He is the smartest, has the most money, and has the power to make everything happen. He is a father who can do anything in the world." How happy would a child with such a father be?

When we say that our Father is the best, God also says, "Oh, that's right! That's right!" and He is happy.

Are you all like that? Even if you were a famous person who painted pictures in the past, you would want to keep everything you did well from elementary school as a relic, right? If you have a drawing that your teacher praised, you would want to keep it and show it off to someone. Isn't that right? Those with good voices want to sing, but when they sing, they want to do it in front of someone they like, not someone they dislike. Therefore, when someone who sings well finds themselves in a relative environment where they can interact, they get excited and want to sing. Isn't that true? There may be someone like that here. Just having something good makes you want to show it off.

Why is that? It is because you want to give and take in a relative relationship. Among the things to give and take, what is the most precious? It is giving and receiving love.

The relationship between a parent and child is something that cannot be severed by anyone. The relationship of a parent and child connects to eternity, and no one can revolutionize it. Who can revolutionize the genuine love between a parent and child? "Hey, you shouldn't have the same loving heart for your child as before!" Even if you mobilize a million troops of the world and threaten them, will that change anything? If there is a loving husband and a loving wife, and you say, "Get rid of all that love! You cannot love!" and threaten them, outwardly it may show, but inwardly, their hearts will burn even more.
That is love. Isn't it? In this love, there is something strong and internal that cannot be revolted against or stopped by human power. But that doesn't mean it's a bad thing. The more you do it, the better it gets. 

Now, what is that? It is love. From that perspective, God is also similar to humans. Because He resembles humans, what does God love? He loves His sons and daughters immensely. Not only does He love them, but He also desires to live together with them. This is a natural principle. 

Then, what would have happened if Adam and Eve had not fallen in Eden and had lived according to God's will? They would have undoubtedly become sons and daughters who could live with God and would have lived well. Would they have lived poorly or well? "They would have lived well." They would have lived well. That's what it means. 

So, what does it mean to live well? Is it living apart, with one person going east and the other going west? No, it means living together. Together... This phrase is really nice. We must live together. If one goes east, the other goes east too. If one goes to heaven, the other goes to heaven too. In a Korean song, there is a line that goes "Oh, my love!" What does that "Oh" mean? (The recording cuts off briefly.) 

Only God can govern, only God can relate... Isn't that so? Does love prefer two people to relate? What do you think? Love... When a mother and father are together, and when they have many children, the mother and father often meet and strategize. They call each other and say, "Hey! Hey! I love you the most." (Laughter) It's the same. It's all the same. Because God is the same, He cannot separate from Adam and Eve. 

In that love, where God is happy and smiling, is there anyone who would say, "Hey, God!" and try to stop it? Is there anyone who would dare to say, "No!" to the omniscient and omnipotent God who is smiling with flowers blooming on His face? 

When God is happy, how do His sons and daughters react? Do they think, "Dad is a bit strange?" No, the children also smile. When they are happy, they smile. It's the same. 

Now, when God is smiling... Everyone, where does a smile begin? Where does it start? Think about it. Where does a smile start? Does it start from the nose, the mouth, or the eyes? "It starts from the eyes." Yes, it starts from the eyes. (Laughter) Why does it start from the eyes? Because creation began with the eyes. Since they came into being first, the essence must all be mobilized to smile. If only part of it smiles... Therefore, the emotion of smiling is seen through the mouth. Isn't that so? (Making expressions) This also seems like a smile... (Laughter) I don't know. But if you look at the eyes, it shows that one is smiling. This is all logical. 

That's why when animals are born, or when baby birds are born, it's the same. If you break an egg in a nest, the eyes appear first. Frogs are the same. When you see tadpoles, the eyes appear first. Isn't that right? The eyes must be happy first, and then the tail will also become happy. Therefore, when smiling, what must start smiling first? The eyes must smile first. 

Then, why are there two eyes? Because God is made with two eyes. In our Unification Church terminology, we can say, "One is a plus eye, and one is a minus eye; this is why there are two." 

So, when one eye smiles, can the other eye not smile? (Laughter) God is a duality of masculine and feminine. But can the plus aspect smile while the minus aspect holds back? (Laughter) No, it cannot. When the plus aspect smiles, the minus aspect automatically follows. "Hey, you plus aspect, start smiling! Hey, minus aspect, start smiling!" (Laughter) There is no mechanism that can hold back the entire universe when that happens. When one smiles, the other must smile as well. Isn't that right? "Yes." 

Also, what do the eyes symbolize? They symbolize God. They symbolize the God of the universe. 

The harmony of heaven and earth cannot be achieved unilaterally. 

Also, the nose symbolizes Adam and Eve. That's right. Why does the nose symbolize Adam and Eve? Because when you breathe in, you become one. The foremost guide of the universe is the nose. It is at the very front. Isn't that so? It is at the very front. Therefore, the foremost guide of the universe is Adam and Eve. The phrase "to pierce the nose" is quite interesting. When someone says, "That guy has been pierced in the nose," it means they have been completely governed. When we say someone can govern, we say they can pierce the nose, right? Isn't that so? There is a common understanding here. 

So, these two nostrils are meant to come together and become one. They are meant to unite. But if one nostril is blocked, do you feel good? (Laughter) When you have a cold and one nostril is blocked, you want to clear it, right? (Laughter) It must be cleared for you to feel good! Isn't that so? That's how it is.

Formalization of the education system (training sessions)

By doing this, on the day people come for short-term training, they can usually get through the first week easily. Then it becomes ten days. After that, how can we ensure that they enter the 21-day training after a week? All the beds in the accommodation have numbers. That number becomes that person’s number. For the one-week training, if someone has number one, after finishing the one-week training and packing up to enter the three-week training, that number will follow them. If that person cannot receive the three-week training, then another person will take over that number. If someone started with number one, that number will continue to follow them through the 40-day training and the 6-month training.

And how did we organize this? We made it so that those who receive the 21-day training are together with those who are in the 7-day training. Also, those in the 40-day training are placed with those in the three-week training, and we try to keep them together with those in the previous stages of training. This way, the person who received the one-week training becomes a senior. So, as a senior, they promote the three-week training. They say the three-week training is really good and that everyone must take it. Then, those who have completed the three-week training are also made to be together with the 40-day trainees. There are two beds in each room, so four people can stay together. This is how we have set it up. One person is a 40-day trainee, and one person is a 21-day trainee, so we can always accommodate those coming in for the one-week training.

Therefore, as soon as they enter the one-week training, they will already know everything about the 21-day training and the 40-day training within that week. This is quite effective. Among those who came for the 3-day training, 93% transition to the one-week training. Almost everyone transitions. This shows that there is effectiveness. Then, among those who finish the one-week training, 78% enter the 21-day training. This is a significant achievement. In the past, it was less than one-third, but now it exceeds two-thirds. After that, starting from January 10, we will transition to the 40-day training course. We expect that at least 70% will transition to this 40-day course. This way, we want to train them as much as possible up to the 40-day training and then utilize them.

Once they receive the 40-day training, they generally reach the stage where they are ready to dedicate their lives for the purpose. Excitement, interest, and effort of trainees in economic activities
So far, when I brought people to train in Japan, I instructed them to organize like this, and they completed the 21-day training. That ended on December 28. After that, they engage in economic activities.

Therefore, after receiving the one-week training, if they engage in economic activities for just one day, they leave with everything earned. (Laughter) So, there is no problem. After finishing the one-week training, we officially have them go out for economic activities. However, those who had not studied are already sitting for ten days. When they come back, there is a lot to talk about. So, after completing the one-week training and engaging in economic activities for just one day, the next step is the three-week training.
For one day, we just feed them. For three weeks, we feed them, but we only engage them in economic activities once a week. This three-week course is really interesting. During the three weeks of study, after finishing one week, when they go out to engage in economic activities, they get really excited. As they continue studying, they want to go out into the city and get some fresh air. Thinking about studying for one week, two weeks, and three weeks makes them feel frustrated, so they just want to go out. When asked, 'Do you want to study or do you want to engage in economic activities?' everyone says, 'Economic activities!' (laughter) They have all been competing since the one-week training. Do you understand? Since over 70 percent of the colleagues who trained together during the one-week training have come up, they are competing again. They say, 'I lost last time, but this time I will win,' and they make bets with each other.

As a result, on the days they go out for economic activities, those people get very excited and wake up early in the morning. (laughs) They are like this. With this, the performance in economic activities during the 21-day course increases by over 30 percent. When comparing the percentage of economic activities after the one-week training and the number of economic activities after entering the three-week training, the number of economic activities in the three-week training averages over 30 percent higher. Do you understand what I mean? They think of it as exciting and they have that much confidence and effort. By the time the 21-day training is over, they think, 'Making money is this easy!' They realize that they have to work like a dog in the company for a month to earn $700, but going out and engaging in activities, earning $100 a day is not a problem at all. Because of this, they say, 'What is that company?' (laughter) They go to work to make money, but after experiencing that making money is not an issue, they plan to quit the company altogether. Then they say, 'Let's go into the 40-day training.'

As a result, no matter where they are, there are seniors and juniors, so juniors follow seniors and an automatic organizational structure is formed.

If a person who has received 21-day training and a person who has received 40-day training are together, when they meet, who can lead? Do you think that is easy? It is easy to watch, but those who play the main role must engage in fierce struggles. Dozens of issues arise in a day. They know that as fun. Do you understand? "Yes."
If there is no money, there is the fun of making money... I am giving a special order to do such work. So, I do it at night, and I travel a thousand miles. Do it, do it! Do it like this! If we do such a war in Korea... Korea is too small to touch, in fact. We need to cook the world. Do you understand? "Yes." Our mission is to seize the world. We should not look at the ground below. Even if we get a wife, even if we get married, it is the same. (The recording cuts off for a moment)
So even Elijah said, "Am I the only one left?" If you just want to sleep, sleep, and if you want to eat, eat, that won't do. If you are responsible for a problem, you must bear that problem. You must persuade when it's time to persuade, and you must engage in diplomacy when it's time for diplomacy. You must know how to make money. You must know how to engage in diplomacy, how to earn money, how to give persuasive speeches to the public, and how to mobilize the public. Therefore, you need to know that such training is necessary. Do you understand? "Yes."
How many tears have you shed for the purpose? Thinking of the purpose, centered on the deep heart of heaven, I need only your strength; the world may not know you, but I alone need your strength... You must also engage in the suffocating close combat of receiving confirmation. If you have received a command, in carrying out that command, even if it means breaking yourself into pieces, do not try to turn back, but go straight ahead. Be a man and break beautifully.
Miracles are happening in America now. God's will is for the world... How do we establish a tradition that can leave this will as the will of all mankind? We must leave at least one step of the tradition. Even if everything in the Unification Church disappears, this path of tradition must remain. How do we leave a tradition that can make even a stone-hearted man shed tears, stand upright, look up to heaven, and reflect on himself when he encounters that tradition? When that is left, even if history flows, when this appears as a tradition before all people, a nation will move, and when a nation moves, a whole world will undoubtedly move. If you have made such a commitment... This applies everywhere.
When you go to the company, instead of saying, "I worked for eight hours, so I will leave," you should say you will work at least double that for eight hours. You should treat this work as your own and say you will work 24 hours. "The pay is only a third, but I cannot work in proportion to my pay. I do not live to be indebted. I live to give back." You should say that. It applies to the church, to the country, and to the world... That is not an easy task.
If you know these principles and become those who can transcend the boundaries of life and death, you will never fail. Why? Because I have said so, because I know that the God I serve is undoubtedly real... Even in this UN issue, I said, "If Korea listens to me and does as I say this time, Korea will definitely win. If it doesn't work, then God does not exist." Do you think they will listen to that? When the UN General Assembly is held, only the elites of the world gather. I mobilized the young women to dance and gathered them for about a week. They gained confidence. When I did it, it turned out to be nothing. I am leading by being at the forefront. When that happens, I can relieve God's resentment.
That is why even if it is past midnight or past two o'clock, I cannot be tired even if I stay up all night. I must be loyal in this position. Even now, I didn't sleep much last night. Did I sleep for an hour? Look. From the standpoint of being responsible for someone else's life... With the crucial marriage issue that happens only once in a lifetime... If I make a mistake, that family could perish, and that generation could perish... It is serious.
Even if I choose in an instant, it is better than you taking decades to choose. If I see it as certain, it is certain. That is why I am doing this. It is serious. I must carry out the mission of a leader that does not exist in the world with a fortune that is bound to fail. The teacher knew that secret, which is why the Unification Church has not failed but has developed and won, and I can put up this sign. Do you understand? "Yes." Do not be a coward.
The teacher's marriage is the same. If you look at the teacher himself, at 40 years old, he married a girl who was 18. Because the teacher, who had the responsibility to move this great organization, needed a supporter, he chose a woman who had graduated from college, but he chose his mother. Because the path was such, he needed someone who would not assert herself and could sacrifice her life for her husband even in the face of death. That is why he never chose the daughter of someone who shakes their head.
The daughter of someone who silently sacrifices from the bottom and resolves to go is the one chosen. That is why he chose the daughter of a woman who was dedicated to the church, a daughter who was in the second year of high school. Why? Because it was the providential principle. Even when obtaining a wife, it was not based on his own desires. There was a principled standard that it must be before the age of 20...
He has been doing such things until now. He has abandoned his family, and he has faced opposition from the nation for the sake of the purpose. He faces opposition from established churches, but just wait and see. They will fail and come to me, saying, "Please help, Mr. Moon." That is how the world works. The path of good and evil goes through a fair judgment process centered on a crossroads. That is how good advances, and that is how heaven guides us to reach that destination.
You must always shed tears and sweat, sacrificing your flesh and blood for the nation and the world, and you must be those who joyfully acknowledge that. Therefore, you must receive training in your direct life. You must overcome. Do you understand? "Yes."
<Prayer> Beloved Father, I know that the Unification Church's Mr. Moon is an extremely weak man. I have long realized that I am one of the most foolish people in the world. I have discovered that the weak me, who has gone through your name, has a way to be strong without losing to anyone in the world because of you. Father, even though I stand in such a weak position, I have been able to stand strong centered on your will, knowing you, knowing your will, and knowing how you have come through the historical process. 
Father, when starting the first seven-year course, when I told foolish people that after ten years it should be like this, I seemed like a madman. No one believed me. However, because you are alive, the absurd and unbelievable facts have come to this day, having risen to a global level. I cannot help but sincerely congratulate you, the living and marvelous Father, who has led us to this point.
Father, the past three years have been a period of fierce struggle in America. From the day you announced the final battle for humanity, with both hands and arms spread...
사람이냐? 나라를 위해 태어나고, 나라를 위해 살고, 나라를 위해 목숨을 다하는 사람이 참된 애국자라고 할 수 있습니다. 그렇게 되어야만 그 나라는 이상적인 국가로서 존재할 수 있고, 국민들 앞에 진정으로 사랑받는 국가가 될 수 있습니다.

이와 같은 원칙을 통해 우리는 모든 존재가 서로를 위해 존재해야 한다는 사실을 깨닫게 됩니다. 사랑, 이상, 행복, 평화는 결코 혼자서는 이룰 수 없는 것임을 이해해야 합니다. 우리는 서로를 위해 존재하며, 서로를 위해 사랑하고, 서로를 위해 행복을 추구해야 합니다.

이제 여러분에게 한 가지 질문을 드리고 싶습니다. 여러분은 과연 누군가를 위해 존재하고 있습니까? 여러분의 삶이 누군가를 위해 헌신하고, 그들을 위해 사랑하고, 그들을 위해 행복을 추구하는 삶이 되고 있습니까? 만약 그렇지 않다면, 여러분의 삶은 진정한 의미를 잃게 될 것입니다.

사랑과 행복은 상대적입니다. 우리가 누군가를 위해 존재할 때, 우리는 진정한 사랑과 행복을 느낄 수 있습니다. 그러므로 우리는 서로를 위해 존재해야 하며, 서로를 위해 사랑해야 합니다. 이것이 우리가 추구해야 할 삶의 원칙입니다.

오늘 저녁 이 자리에 함께한 여러분이 이러한 원칙을 마음에 새기고, 서로를 위해 존재하는 삶을 살아가기를 바랍니다. 여러분의 삶이 누군가에게 사랑과 행복을 주는 삶이 되기를 기원합니다. 감사합니다.
Are you a person? If you ask this question, you cannot help but mention figures like General Yi Sun-sin, who was born for the country, lived for the country, and selflessly sacrificed his life for the country, regardless of the difficult circumstances, for the king above and for the people below.

If we broaden the scope to the world and ask who is the greatest saint in the historical journey, we can quickly find that person by applying this principle. That person must be one who lived for humanity more than anyone else. Many who attended here may not believe in Christianity, but as far as I know, Jesus Christ, who came for humanity, died for humanity, and even prayed for his enemies, whom he should rightfully hate, is undoubtedly the greatest of saints in history. This conclusion can be drawn through this principle. We must consider that the principle of the creation of the universe and the origin of human happiness begins with 'existing for others.'

If I give another example and ask why a man was born, many people here today, including prominent figures, might easily think that a man was born for himself, to not lose to anyone in the Republic of Korea. Men have likely thought that they were born because of other men. However, the original intention behind a man's birth is that he was born because of women. This fact that he was born because of women cannot be denied by anyone.

From a relative perspective, men have broad shoulders, while women have broader hips. When you go to a crowded subway in New York, you can see that when a broad-shouldered man and a broad-hipped woman sit together in a cramped seat, they fit perfectly. Even when we see such things, we cannot deny that they were born to establish a relative relationship where they can care for each other. Men were not born because of men, but because of women. Conversely, women were not born because of women, but because of men.

We must understand that problems arise when we cannot be confident in these facts. This is because God, the great ruler of creation, established the principle of creation, and I believe that without following that principle, we cannot enter a good, true, happy, peaceful world, or a world of love and ideals.

The teachings of religion are aligned with the laws of the original world. You may not know this well, but I have had many opportunities to experience spiritual experiences, that is, to understand the spiritual world. If you ask what the structure of the original world where God exists, which is referred to today as heaven or paradise, is based on, the answer is simple. It is a place where those who exist for God can enter, where those who are born for others, live for others, and die for others can enter. This is the ideal structure of our homeland, and that is why God has established numerous religions throughout history to train humanity to come to that world.

Why must religious people be humble and sacrifice? It is because that is the law of the homeland. In preparation for the time when they will return to their homeland, they must be trained in their earthly lives to fit that homeland, which is why higher religions emphasize greater sacrifice and service. They cannot help but emphasize this to align with that world.

When we consider these facts, we cannot help but acknowledge that the process of history is governed by God. No matter how vast the Bible is, it all fits into the two words: 'exist for others.'

Jesus said, "Whoever wants to be exalted must be humbled, and whoever wants to be humbled will be exalted." This paradoxical statement is merely a means to align with the principle of 'existing for others' in the original world.

So why did God have to establish the principle of existing for others? Let me present a few reasons. When we reflect on our true intentions, if there is someone to whom we owe our lives, our true heart would want to repay that debt not just 100%, but more than 100%. In other words, if person A owes person B 100%, B would want to repay A more than 100%. Then A would want to repay B with an even higher percentage. In this exchange, the more the exchange increases, the more it grows, which is where the concept of eternity is established.

The concept of eternity is impossible when it comes to existing for oneself. Even in observing movement, the greater the relative direction of pushing and pulling, the faster it spins.

God, who is the king of wisdom, established the law to exist for others to make it eternal. We must think that because He knows this principle, He could not help but establish the principle of existing for others.

Moreover, with the establishment of the concept of eternity, it leads to eternal advancement and prosperity. It means progressing and developing from the current position. One must be able to feel a progressive stimulus from their current position to be happy. Because of these requirements, God could not help but establish the principle of existing for others.

Another reason why the principle of existing for others had to be established is this: Suppose there are ten family members in a household. If the youngest sibling lives for the entire family, even though they are young, the parents and siblings will elevate them. As time goes on, that sibling, who exists for the family, will automatically emerge as the central figure of that household.

Since God created this universe and exists for others, just as He is the central being of the universe, a person who resembles God, even if they are a young sibling or the youngest son, will undoubtedly take on a central position in their lineage. Today, we did not realize this.

In living for others, one does not retreat; rather, the more one serves others, the more they become a central being, just like God. Because God is like that, a person who stands in such a position cannot help but be established as a central being by God. Moreover, only in such a position can ideal unity and complete unity be achieved.

Today, we know that there are many people who cannot stand being governed by others. This is especially evident among the educated elite. However, one thing we must understand is how happy it is to live under the governance of one who exists for others, a fact they have never even considered.

When we look at the organization of the spiritual world, God, who is the great ruler of heaven and earth, is the central being who exists for others among all beings in the universe. Therefore, they do not realize how happy it is to be governed by Him. Even if they were to be governed for a thousand or ten thousand years, they would be grateful because they know that such an ideal unified realm is established in such a position, which is why God could not help but establish the principle of existing for others.

Another reason is that today you think, "Love is my love. Ideals are my ideals." But that is not the case. Love did not start from me, nor did ideals start from me. Where can we find love and ideals that are more precious than life? Only in the object; without the object, they cannot be found. Today, we have not considered this.

The existence that can receive and seek this noble love and ideals is the object. Therefore, to humbly accept this noble love and ideals, we must stand in the position that serves others. Without doing so, we cannot receive this, which is why God could not help but establish the principle of existing for others. I hope that everyone here tonight remembers this fact.

Often in the world, people say, "Ah! What is life? What is life?" Similarly, for us humans, establishing a view of life, a view of the nation, a view of the world, and further, establishing a view of the universe and a view of God becomes an issue. How did this happen? The question of where to place the order of systematic stages and how to connect the dimensional series is the most serious issue.

A new value system based on existing for others must be established. Based on the principle of existing for others, when we look at our lives, the most valuable view of life is that I exist for all humanity, for the whole world, for the nation, for society, for my family, for my wife, and for my children. If we can discover a happy self from this perspective, there is no higher view of life than this.

The same goes for the nation itself. What should an ideal nation be like? We can see through history that a nation that exists only for itself is condemned as a bad nation. However, among the nations of the world today, there is not a single nation that is pursuing policies for the world.

As you know, today’s communism is entering a state of collapse. What was the cause of the split in communism around 1957? It was because communism centered around the Soviet Union dreamed of world domination based on a single Slavic ethnicity. We know that the split occurred because it emerged as a communism that only served its own ethnicity.

Today, we are witnessing the reality that the United States is also declining from its position as the leading democratic nation. Why? Because it has become a country that tries to serve only itself while abandoning the world, instead of becoming a democratic nation that serves the world. Now, the United States, which is on the path of retreat, has no way to recover on its own.

When we look at these issues, we see that today in Korea, if a national perspective is established that focuses only on Korea in Asia, it will flow away with the tide of history. The Soviet Communist Party was like that, and we can see that the United States itself has been like that. If today, the Republic of Korea, despite being a small and minority nation, has a national ideology that serves the world, even if its form disappears, in the 21st, 25th, or 30th century, Korea will surely lead the world. We can conclude this as an official result.

Then, a true nation is one that serves the world. Moreover, a true world does not serve only the world. Since that world itself is in a position of result, if there is an absolute God who is the origin of the motive, there must be an ideological system that can align with that God’s perspective. It is believed that one cannot lead and resolve the world with an ideology that serves oneself.

There is nothing that does not connect with the principle of existing for others. If you ask what a heavenly family is like… when a wife exists 100% for her husband, and the husband lives for her and dies for her, that family cannot be anything but heaven.

There is a saying in our proverbs: "Harmony in the family brings success in everything." The same goes for a nation. The sovereign who governs a nation must realize that the value of their existence is not in exercising their sovereignty, but in serving the people, and that the people must serve the nation rather than themselves. When that day comes, that nation will become heaven.

By expanding such official principles, if we can create a world where nations and ethnicities transcend each other and serve one another, that world will undoubtedly be the utopian world of love, the world of ideals, the world of peace, and the world of happiness that we humans desire. There is no place where the principle of existing for others does not apply.

What was the motivation behind my ability to raise issues in a short period when I went to America? It was because I loved America more than Americans, even though I am Korean. Day and night, I worked hard to ensure that the youth of America could have noble ideals, pouring my blood and sweat for this nation. The only thing I have done is to live for others, to act for others, and to exist for others. As I have lived this way, I have seen that when I collide with individuals, I become one with them, and when I collide with groups, I harmonize with them.

You may not know this well, but I knew that the Korean issue was in serious trouble at this UN General Assembly. I mobilized all the organizations I knew to gather information. When looking at the evaluations from the chair of the UN General Assembly, his assistants, and the ambassadors and observers from various countries, it was decisively clear that there was already no hope for the Korean issue.

Until now, I have personally believed that as a religious leader or as a leader of the Unification Church, the Unification Church should not exist just for itself; it must exist for the nation, and not only for the nation but must guide it to be a nation that can lead the world. I believed that no explanation or propaganda was necessary.

I gathered missionaries from over 30 countries and elected representatives from 34 countries. I then paired them with 34 Japanese women, sending a total of 68 members to the UN General Assembly. I engaged in one-on-one persuasion with each person.

What was the content? It was nothing special. It was not about speaking well. I told them, "With all your sincerity, serve them! From the moment you meet, from eating together to talking, strive to serve them." After 40 days of this effort, they were impressed by our activities.

As a responsible leader of religion, I believed that no matter how unfavorable the world’s opinion of Korea was, the day we received signatures from ambassadors of 50 countries to promote the free movement of Japanese wives would surely lead to victory for the Korean issue. (Applause)

When I said this, they did not believe it. The UN General Assembly is where the world's intellectuals gather. Our young people did not have the confidence to dare to speak to them. However, those who sincerely serve others…
Centering on the run position... Knowing that place not as an office of some country or someone, but as my home office, I would go there and provide small tasks, and if it was something that could help them until late at night, I would mobilize my car without caring about the time. This is the kind of activity that I developed behind the scenes. As you all know, we have our guesthouse in a place called Tarrytown. Centered around a place called Belvedere, I invited ambassadors from 70 countries at night. As I engaged in these activities, they eventually began to completely side with us.

Through this process, I learned that North Korea had already decided to sign at the UN General Assembly with countries in the Third World, specifically in underdeveloped regions like Africa. Summarizing the contents of what they secretly stated, North Korea had already paid amounts ranging from $50,000 to $150,000 and had come to a decision. I learned that Kim Il-sung himself raised a toast to the delegation he was sending to the UN and dispatched them.

However, the result after conveying the heartfelt stories of serving the world, shedding tears, and staying up all night was that in the matter of Korea, South Korea's proposal won with 61 votes to 42, while North Korea's proposal was tied at 48 to 48, bringing us victory. I am not sharing this fact to boast in front of you. I have experienced many unimaginable miracles based on this principle throughout my life.

You may wonder... what exactly is the Unification Church? Many theologians have tried to reconcile the split between Roman Catholicism and Greek Orthodoxy throughout history, but they could not achieve that even in their dreams. Many Protestant denominations emerged, but they ended up splitting into over 400 sects. Given this reality, how could the Unification Church possibly unify religions? Is it even possible?

When we look at this, you might think that a person named Moon is somewhat lacking in intelligence, but I see the problem as simple. Can one love the members of established churches more than their pastors? Can Unification Church members love their pastors more than their congregants? If this is possible, then it is indeed possible.

To this day, the Unification Church has a history of 20 years. You may have heard all sorts of rumors and controversies about the Unification Church. The Unification Church has been trampled on the ground, yet it has developed globally. How did it develop? It understood that when a nation betrays, there is a path to the world. The path that a nation must take is the path that goes for the world, which is the right way, and if this path is indeed an undeniable principle of a thousand miles and a common formula for all people, then if the nation does not recognize it, when the world goes on a path that the world can recognize for the world, this nation will inevitably come to know it. Based on this principle, we have expanded our foreign missions amidst bloody persecution.

For example, when I was pioneering Japan, it was 17 years ago during the Liberal Party era. At that time, due to the Ewha Womans University incident, the situation of a person named Moon was terrible, but I had a sense of how the situation in Japan would unfold and how the situation in Asia would develop. Therefore, as a citizen of a law-abiding country, I thought that although it might be illegal at the time, there would come a time within 5 to 10 years when the Republic of Korea would need us, so I felt I had no choice but to pursue this path, even if it meant being branded a criminal. In 1956, as you know, after being released from Seodaemun Prison and while resting at a resort in Gapsa, Chungnam, I called a young man named Choi Bong-chun and instructed him, "You are going to Japan by illegal means. A man must be prepared to face death for the path he has chosen."

At first, he was arrested as soon as he entered Japan. The first attempt ended in failure. I sent him again. The second attempt also failed and he returned. When I came out of prison, the situation of the Unification Church was such that all the churches had disappeared, and even a single room was completely gone, but I borrowed money for the sake of the country and Asia and initiated a third departure. That event feels like it was just yesterday. It was in 1958. The Unification Church in Japan started under such circumstances. On the third attempt, he was also arrested and detained in Omura detention center.

Now, since that happened, Mr. Choi was in big trouble. He had made a solid promise with me, but he was not in a position to lay a foundation; he had become a prisoner, so who could he turn to for help? With nowhere to turn, he pretended to be sick by eating soy sauce and causing a fever. He went through the process of hospitalization and stayed in the hospital for three days before escaping and heading to Tokyo, which is how the current Unification Church in Japan began.

Now, the Liberal Democratic Party of Japan has reached a stage where they request our advice. When they have important national matters, they come to seek out Kuboki, bringing us to that level. Meanwhile, this principle is a principle established by heavenly law. I taught that if we push forward according to this principle, we will not fail. Because we understood this principle, the young male and female members of the Unification Church in Japan spread across the country, saying, "We must become a Unification Church for the nation," "We must become a Unification Church for Asia," and further, "We must become a Unification Church for the world." As they engaged in these activities, they have now become prominent even within Japan.

Today, meeting you in an official setting and sharing these stories is the first time in the 20-year history of the Unification Church. As I traveled across North America, I felt a sense of regret thinking, "This poor man, like an orphan, is in a pitiful position, having to seek faith from foreign nationals while leaving behind juniors in my country who do not believe in me. However, God has raised such a person to work, so the God who cooperates with me will know," and I held on to God and worked hard, and as a result, I experienced the emergence of a new history of creation.

Realizing heaven is only possible through living for others
Today, those of you who are present here may wonder how to measure who is a wicked person and who is a good person. However, it is simple. No matter how religious a person may be, how can we measure whether they will go to heaven or hell? If a person has lived a life for themselves, they are heading to hell. If a person has lived a life for others that is even 1 percent more than a life lived for themselves, they are standing on the path that can lead them to heaven beyond hell. However, when the proportion of their life lived for themselves is high, they are going to hell.

Esteemed teachers! Until now, we have contributed to this country as members of the Republic of Korea. Each of us has contributed from our respective positions, but for whom was that? When all citizens revolutionize in this way across various fields, no matter how miserable the Republic of Korea may be, there is hope for the Republic of Korea. This applies in families, in society, from politicians, or from leaders of organizations. When the spirit and culture of this nation become such, this nation will absolutely not perish. This nation will inevitably influence Asia and the world.

From this perspective, if I were to conclude how we can find an ideal system through a single formula, it would be that husbands live for their wives, wives live for their husbands, and that couples live for their children. Families live for their clans, clans live for their nations, nations live for their countries, and countries live for the world. When a nation can live for the world, that nation will not perish.

If God exists, He demands such people. God wants to make all humanity His children. Therefore, God's purpose is to save humanity. Furthermore, it is to save the universe. A religion that cannot shed the guise of a single nation or ethnic group cannot stand before God's overall will.

Since God's main purpose is to save the world, when we think about how to develop the possible dimensions that can achieve that, the principle is simple. Families exist for clans, clans exist for nations, nations exist for countries, countries exist for the world, and the world exists for God. Only those who live for the world are qualified to become children of the omnipotent God who created the entire universe. If the world stands in a position to serve God, then God stands in a position to serve the world, to serve the nation, to serve the ethnic group, and to serve the family.

To put this in other words, what is mine is my wife's; what belongs to the couple is the family's; what belongs to the family is the clan's; what belongs to the clan is the nation's; what belongs to the nation is the country's; and what belongs to the country is the world's. The world that holds this concept ultimately becomes God's. If it is God's, then whose is it? It becomes mine. Only by advancing to such a position can you stand in a place where your desires are maximally fulfilled. Everyone, isn't that true? Everyone has a desire to be the best in the world. Because of this valuable existence, humans can finally stand in a glorious position where God's things become their own.

In conclusion, realizing heaven through living for others is possible for family heaven, national heaven, and world heaven. Furthermore, God will also connect to a world where He can be happy and dance and sing with humanity, which is the world that religion aims for. Since that heaven is realized on earth, it leads to the conclusion that this is indeed the earthly heaven.

Through this banquet today, I have shared the principle of "living for others" with you. Now, as you return to your homes, workplaces, or schools, I hope you can be those who can embody this principle. When you discover yourself living this way, you will have a brighter hope for the future and will surely recognize your central responsibility as a pioneer for tomorrow.

I sincerely hope that you can be such individuals, and may God's blessings be even more abundant in your families, societies, and this nation. I have conveyed the message of living for others this evening. Now, I will conclude my remarks. (Applause)
